***stroef.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stroef.html>stroef</a> (43000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">struuf</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*strūf</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*strūbaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiff.html>stiff</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rough.html>rough</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bristly.html>bristly</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:shaggy.html>shaggy</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*strewbʰ-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*strewb-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stiff.html>stiff</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">struuf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language"><a href = vnd.unilang:west.html>West</a> Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:stroef.html>stroef</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">straub</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">struppig</i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stront.html>stront</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a>, dreck, <a href = vnd.unilang:manure.html>manure</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*strunt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:excrement.html>excrement</a>, turd, <a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:you.html>You</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:can.html>can</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:help.html>help</a> Wiktionary <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> elaborating <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> origins <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a>.</i></span>

***struisvogel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogel.html>struisvogel</a> (42998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struis.html>struis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ostrich.html>ostrich</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vogel.html>vogel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bird.html>bird</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Attested <a href = vnd.unilang:since.html>since</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 17th <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>, displacing earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vogelstruis</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:element.html>element</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struis.html>struis</a></i> derives <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">strūthiō</i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:struisvogel.html>struisvogel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ostrich.html>ostrich</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:politiek.html>politiek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:politics.html>politics</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:possibly.html>possibly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> calque <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> calque <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a>  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vogel-Strauß-Politik</i>. Named <a href = vnd.unilang:after.html>after</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:common.html>common</a> misconception <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> ostriches <a href = vnd.unilang:bury.html>bury</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:their.html>their</a> heads <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sand.html>sand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:when.html>when</a> confronted <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:danger.html>danger</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>First</a> attested <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> 1848.

***stuffy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuffy.html>stuffy</a> (28465)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuffy.html>stuffy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">stuffier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">stuffiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Poorly ventilated; <a href = vnd.unilang:partially.html>partially</a> plugged.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stucke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stuc</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stukki</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stukkiją</i>.
